    \theutterance \stepcounter{utterance}  

    & & & \multicolumn{2}{p{0.3\linewidth}}{\cellcolor[rgb]{0.95,0.95,0.95}{%
	\makecell[{{p{\linewidth}}}]{% 
	  \tt {\tiny [GM$|$GM]}  
	 {'goal_states_achieved': ['on(mop1,table1)', 'on(plate1,table1)', 'on(book1,table1)'], 'game_successfully_finished': True} 
	  } 
	   } 
	   } 
	 & & \\ 
 

\end{supertabular}
}
